RUS_voskhod_decisions = {
	RUS_increase_funding = {
		icon = GFX_decision_hol_attract_foreign_investors
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		visible = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_voskhod_active
		}
		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		cost = 40
		days_remove = 14
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 10000
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = RUS_did_increase_funding_decision
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_republic_ai
					has_country_flag = RUS_empire_ai
					has_country_flag = RUS_socialist_ai
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel RUS_increase_funding"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_political_power = 40
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_increase_funding"
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_voskhod_cap = 50000
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 50000
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_increase_voskhod_50000_tt
			RUS_check_voskhod_recruit = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_did_increase_funding_decision
			}
		}
	}
	RUS_utilise_army = {
		icon = GFX_decision_soldierly_discipline

				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {

			}

			}

			}

				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			}
			562 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			}
			409 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			}
			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = RUS_power_balance
				value = 0.05
			}

	RUS_norilsk_mining_and_metallurgy = {
		icon = steel
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}

		}
		visible = {

		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 80
		}
		highlight_states = {
			highlight_state_targets = {
				state = 516
			}
		}
		#Taymyr
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete RUS_norilsk_mining_and_metallurgy target: [From.GetName]"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_manpower = -50000
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_voskhod_current_mp = 50000
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_voskhod_total_mp = 50000
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 50000
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_norilsk_mining_and_metallurgy target: [From.GetName]"
			subtract_from_variable = {
				RUS_voskhod_current_mp = 50000
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_voskhod_remaining_mp = 50000
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_completed_voskhod_projects = 1
			}
			RUS_check_voskhod_events = yes
			add_resource = {
				type = steel
				amount = 30
				state = 516
			}
			add_resource = {
				type = chromium
				amount = 24
				state = 516
			}
			RUS_decrease_black_monday = yes
		}
	}

RUS_ongoing_election = {
	RUS_election_timer = {
		icon = GFX_decision_SWI_swiss_democratic_tradition_campaign
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		#manually activated
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		selectable_mission = yes
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout RUS_election_timer"
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_kadet_var
						value = RUS_PSR_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_kadet_var
						value = RUS_VPP_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_kadet_var
						value = RUS_RDP_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_kadet_victory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_PSR_var
						value = RUS_kadet_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_PSR_var
						value = RUS_VPP_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_PSR_var
						value = RUS_RDP_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_PSR_victory
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_RDP_var
						value = RUS_kadet_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_RDP_var
						value = RUS_VPP_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = RUS_RDP_var
						value = RUS_PSR_var
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_RDP_victory
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = RUS_VPP_victory
			}
			country_event = ruselections.30
		}
	}
}

RUS_sulimov_decisions = {
	RUS_rightwing_obscurantism = {
		icon = GFX_decision_eng_ally_imperialist_coup

			always = no

		#manually activated
		available = {

		}

		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				RUS_sulimov = no
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout RUS_rightwing_obscurantism"
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_stability = -0.025
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						RUS_right_anger > 9
					}
					NOT = {
						has_active_mission = RUS_looming_military_coup
					}
				}
				country_event = demrus.103
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = {
					RUS_anger_change = 1
				}
				RUS_change_right_anger = yes
			}
			activate_mission = RUS_rightwing_obscurantism
		}
	}

								has_character = MON_roman_von_ungern_sternberg

				}

			}

				}
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = RUS_looming_military_coup
					days = 90
				}
			}

RUS_maklakov_decisions = {
	RUS_political_apathy = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_inflation
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		#manually activated
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_path
						option = RUS_PATH_DOLGORUKOV_MARLIB
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_path
						option = RUS_PATH_KARTASHYOV_MARLIB
					}
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = RUS_coalition_of_idealists
			has_country_flag = RUS_law_on_freedoms
		}
		selectable_mission = yes
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 120
		fixed_random_seed = no
		cancel_trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = GER
				RUS_maklakov = no
			}
		}
		cancel_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision cancel RUS_political_apathy"
			clear_variable = RUS_apathy_var
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete RUS_political_apathy"
			clear_variable = RUS_apathy_var
			RUS_increase_democracy = yes
			set_temp_variable = {
				ideology_change_var = 10
			}
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
			add_war_support = 0.1
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_targeted_decision = {
					decision = RUS_pass_progressive_legislation
					target = ROOT
				}
				remove_targeted_decision = {
					decision = RUS_maklakov_resign
					target = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout RUS_political_apathy"
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						RUS_apathy_var < 0
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					RUS_apathy_var = 0
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_apathy_tt
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_apathy_var = 1
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				RUS_apathy_temp = RUS_apathy_var
			}
			divide_temp_variable = {
				RUS_apathy_temp = -100
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				ideology_change_var = RUS_apathy_temp
			}
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
			add_war_support = RUS_apathy_temp
			activate_mission = RUS_political_apathy
		}
	}
	RUS_pass_progressive_legislation = {
		icon = GFX_decision_scales
		cancel_trigger = {
			RUS_rikhter = no
		}
		cost = 50
		days_remove = 60
		cancel_trigger = {
			RUS_maklakov = no
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = {
					RUS_apathy_var < 5
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_path
						option = RUS_PATH_DOLGORUKOV_MARLIB
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_path
						option = RUS_PATH_KARTASHYOV_MARLIB
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_pass_progressive_legislation"
			add_stability = 0.02
			add_to_variable = {

			}

		}

			NOT = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_banking_act
			}
			has_stability > 0.5
		}

		is_good = no

			OR = {
				has_war_with = GER
				RUS_solonevich = no
			}

			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			set_temp_variable = {
				RUS_anger_change = -1
			}
			RUS_change_right_anger = yes
		}
		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision timeout RUS_VPP_tension"

				limit = {
					has_idea = RUS_party_versus_president

				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_party_versus_president
					add_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_2
				}
			}
			else_if = {

					add_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {

					has_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_3
					add_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_4
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_4
					add_idea = RUS_party_versus_president_5
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = -0.04
				}
			}

				RUS_anger_change = 1
			}
			RUS_change_right_anger = yes
			activate_mission = RUS_VPP_tension
		}

					has_decision = RUS_russia_is_republic

					has_decision = RUS_enshrine_military_role

		}

RUS_sorokin_reforms = {
	RUS_rural_schools_program = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_agriculture
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		cost = 80
		days_remove = 180
		fire_only_once = yes
		modifier = {
			monthly_population = 1
			consumer_goods_factor = 0.1
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 150
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_rural_schools_program"
			add_stability = 0.05

		icon = GFX_decision_hand_grab
		allowed = {

		}
		#activated by effect
		visible = {

			}

			FROM = {
				random_core_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 2
						arms_factory > 2
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
				random_core_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 2
						arms_factory > 2
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
				random_core_state = {
					limit = {
						industrial_complex > 2
						arms_factory > 2
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = RUS_looted_state
					remove_building = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
					}
					remove_building = {
						type = industrial_complex
						level = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision remove RUS_industrial_reparations target: [From.GetName]"
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {

						size > 2
					}
				}

					type = arms_factory
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = arms_factory
						size > 1
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 2
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			random_core_state = {
				limit = {
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 1
					}
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

		days_remove = 30

					limit = {

			}
			ROOT = {

					target = FROM

			}

			}
		}
	}

	RUS_restart_war_against_germany = {

			GER
		}

			can_declare_war_on = FROM
		}

		war_with_target_on_remove = yes

			factor = 1000

	### Mine Pilled decision unlocked through Dalzavod MIO
	RUS_dalzavod_mining_baltic_sea = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval_mine
		allowed = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			owns_state = 195
			has_war = yes
		}
		visible = {
			mio:RUS_dalzavod_organisation = {
				is_mio_trait_completed = dalzavod_upgrade_3
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = CP_25
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			NOT = {
				command_power < 25
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 5
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision complete RUS_dalzavod_mining_baltic_sea"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -25
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_mines = {
							region = 272
							amount = 900
						}
					}
				}
				add_mines = {
					region = 272
					amount = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_mines = {
							region = 138
							amount = 900
						}
					}
				}
				add_mines = {
					region = 138
					amount = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_mines = {
					region = 9
					amount = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_variable = RUS_dalzavod_total_mines_launched
					}
				}
				set_variable = {
					RUS_dalzavod_total_mines_launched = 0
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				RUS_dalzavod_total_mines_launched = RUS_dalzavod_mines_number
			}
		}
	}
